## Instruction

Please read the table titled "GDP2022" in Google Sheets and calculate the CR5 index for each of the seven major regions listed by the World Bank. Create a new spreadsheet in Google Sheets, name it "GDP CR5 Analysis", and within it, create a new table titled "gdp_cr5_analysis". Save the following data with headers being `Region`, `Top5_Countries`, `Top5_GDP_Sum`, `Region_GDP_Total`, and `CR5_Ratio`, where they represent the region name, the top five countries (use exactly the full names in existing sheet and separated by "/", from highest to lowest), the sum of the top five countries' GDP, the total regional GDP, and the CR5 index (percentage, rounded to two decimal places). Sort the data in descending order by CR5 index. 

Note: You should strictly following the country classification provided by the World Bank. If one region has less than 5 countries, you just consider the real number of countries in filling the table.

## Initial State

### Google Sheets

The Google Sheet is reinitialized on each test; you can view the original data [here](https://github.com/hkust-nlp/mcpbench_dev/tree/finalpool_dev/tasks/finalpool/gdp-cr5-analysis/preprocess).

<Expandable title="Details">
```python
import json, os

# Paths from overlong outputs
country_path = "/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/UDPZnVQJhsVXvH3Tjbkqzd.json"
region_path = "/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/RAVz9BmNPFoZTnoHXYjTsw.json"
wb_path = "/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/CR6KVDpCib7HjrkBNBtHQr.json"

for p in [country_path, region_path, wb_path]:
    assert os.path.exists(p), f"Missing file: {p}"

# Load JSON
with open(country_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    country_json = json.load(f)
with open(region_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    region_json = json.load(f)
with open(wb_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    wb_json = json.load(f)

# Helper to extract values from Google Sheets row 'values' list

def get_cell_value(cell):
    if not cell:
        return None
    ev = cell.get('effectiveValue') or cell.get('userEnteredValue')
    if not ev:
        return None
    if 'stringValue' in ev:
        return ev['stringValue']
    if 'numberValue' in ev:
        return ev['numberValue']
    if 'boolValue' in ev:
        return ev['boolValue']
    return None

# Parse Country sheet: find header indices
country_rows = country_json['sheets'][0]['data'][0]['rowData']
header_cells = country_rows[0]['values']
headers = [get_cell_value(c) for c in header_cells]
# Map expected headers
try:
    idx_code = headers.index('Country Code')
    idx_name = headers.index('Country Name')
    idx_gdp = headers.index('Economy (millions of US dollars)')
except ValueError as e:
    raise SystemExit(f"Required header not found: {e} in {headers}")

countries = []
for row in country_rows[1:]:
    values = row.get('values', [])
    if not values:
        continue
    code = get_cell_value(values[idx_code]) if idx_code < len(values) else None
    name = get_cell_value(values[idx_name]) if idx_name < len(values) else None
    gdp = get_cell_value(values[idx_gdp]) if idx_gdp < len(values) else None
    if code and name and isinstance(gdp, (int, float)):
        # Skip if code appears to be not ISO3 (e.g., too long/short)
        if not (isinstance(code, str) and len(code) == 3):
            continue
        countries.append({'code': code, 'name': name, 'gdp_musd': float(gdp)})

# Build WB mapping ISO3 -> region id and name
wb_entries = wb_json[1]
iso3_to_region = {}
for entry in wb_entries:
    code = entry.get('id')
    region = entry.get('region', {})
    region_id = region.get('id')
    region_name = region.get('value')
    if code and region_id and region_id in {'EAS','ECS','LCN','MEA','NAC','SAS','SSF'}:
        iso3_to_region[code] = {'region_id': region_id, 'region_name': region_name}

# Filter countries to those present in WB mapping (exclude aggregates or territories outside mapping)
filtered = []
for c in countries:
    if c['code'] in iso3_to_region:
        r = iso3_to_region[c['code']]
        filtered.append({**c, **r})

# Parse Region sheet totals for the 7 major regions
region_rows = region_json['sheets'][0]['data'][0]['rowData']
reg_header_cells = region_rows[0]['values']
reg_headers = [get_cell_value(c) for c in reg_header_cells]
try:
    ridx_code = reg_headers.index('Region Code')
    ridx_name = reg_headers.index('Region Name')
    ridx_gdp = reg_headers.index('Economy (millions of US dollars)')
except ValueError as e:
    raise SystemExit(f"Region header missing: {e} in {reg_headers}")

region_totals = {}
for row in region_rows[1:]:
    values = row.get('values', [])
    if not values:
        continue
    code = get_cell_value(values[ridx_code]) if ridx_code < len(values) else None
    name = get_cell_value(values[ridx_name]) if ridx_name < len(values) else None
    gdp = get_cell_value(values[ridx_gdp]) if ridx_gdp < len(values) else None
    if code in {'EAS','ECS','LCN','MEA','NAC','SAS','SSF'} and isinstance(gdp, (int,float)):
        region_totals[code] = {'name': name, 'gdp_musd': float(gdp)}

# Group countries by region
from collections import defaultdict
by_region = defaultdict(list)
for c in filtered:
    by_region[c['region_id']].append(c)

# Compute CR5 per region
results = []
for code in ['EAS','ECS','LCN','MEA','NAC','SAS','SSF']:
    countries_in_region = by_region.get(code, [])
    countries_in_region.sort(key=lambda x: x['gdp_musd'], reverse=True)
    top = countries_in_region[:5]
    top_names = [c['name'] for c in top]
    top_sum = sum(c['gdp_musd'] for c in top)
    reg_total = region_totals.get(code, {}).get('gdp_musd', 0.0)
    # Name: prefer Region sheet name (to align with spreadsheet), fallback to WB name if missing
    reg_name = region_totals.get(code, {}).get('name') or (countries_in_region[0]['region_name'] if countries_in_region else code)
    cr5_ratio = (top_sum / reg_total * 100.0) if reg_total else 0.0
    results.append({
        'Region': reg_name,
        'Top5_Countries': "/".join(top_names),
        'Top5_GDP_Sum': top_sum,
        'Region_GDP_Total': reg_total,
        'CR5_Ratio': cr5_ratio,
        'region_code': code,
        'country_count': len(countries_in_region)
    })

# Sort by descending CR5 ratio
results.sort(key=lambda x: x['CR5_Ratio'], reverse=True)

# Prepare values for writing
def fmt_pct(x):
    return f"{x:.2f}%"

def fmt_num(x):
    # Keep as number for sheet; but we can also leave raw float; formatting can be applied in sheet later
    return round(x, 3)

headers_out = ['Region','Top5_Countries','Top5_GDP_Sum','Region_GDP_Total','CR5_Ratio']
rows_out = [[
    r['Region'],
    r['Top5_Countries'],
    r['Top5_GDP_Sum'],
    r['Region_GDP_Total'],
    fmt_pct(r['CR5_Ratio'])
] for r in results]

# Also produce a brief debug print
for r in results:
    print(r['region_code'], r['Region'], r['country_count'], fmt_pct(r['CR5_Ratio']))

# Save a local copy of the output just in case
out_path = "/workspace/dumps/workspace/gdp_cr5_results.json"
with open(out_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    json.dump({'headers': headers_out, 'rows': rows_out, 'raw': results}, f, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)
print("Saved:", out_path)
 code

`fetch fetch_json`

<Expandable title="Details">
```python
import json, os

# Paths from overlong outputs
country_path = "/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/UDPZnVQJhsVXvH3Tjbkqzd.json"
region_path = "/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/RAVz9BmNPFoZTnoHXYjTsw.json"
wb_path = "/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/CR6KVDpCib7HjrkBNBtHQr.json"

# Load as text JSON string then parse
with open(country_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    country_outer = json.load(f)
country_json = json.loads(country_outer['text'])

with open(region_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    region_outer = json.load(f)
region_json = json.loads(region_outer['text'])

with open(wb_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    wb_outer = json.load(f)
wb_json = json.loads(wb_outer['text'])

# Helper to extract values from Google Sheets row 'values' list

def get_cell_value(cell):
    if not cell:
        return None
    ev = cell.get('effectiveValue') or cell.get('userEnteredValue')
    if not ev:
        return None
    if 'stringValue' in ev:
        return ev['stringValue']
    if 'numberValue' in ev:
        return ev['numberValue']
    if 'boolValue' in ev:
        return ev['boolValue']
    return None

# Parse Country sheet: find header indices
country_rows = country_json['sheets'][0]['data'][0]['rowData']
header_cells = country_rows[0]['values']
headers = [get_cell_value(c) for c in header_cells]
# Map expected headers
try:
    idx_code = headers.index('Country Code')
    idx_name = headers.index('Country Name')
    idx_gdp = headers.index('Economy (millions of US dollars)')
except ValueError as e:
    raise SystemExit(f"Required header not found: {e} in {headers}")

countries = []
for row in country_rows[1:]:
    values = row.get('values', [])
    if not values:
        continue
    code = get_cell_value(values[idx_code]) if idx_code < len(values) else None
    name = get_cell_value(values[idx_name]) if idx_name < len(values) else None
    gdp = get_cell_value(values[idx_gdp]) if idx_gdp < len(values) else None
    if code and name and isinstance(gdp, (int, float)):
        if not (isinstance(code, str) and len(code) == 3):
            continue
        countries.append({'code': code, 'name': name, 'gdp_musd': float(gdp)})

# Build WB mapping ISO3 -> region id and name
wb_entries = wb_json[1]
iso3_to_region = {}
for entry in wb_entries:
    code = entry.get('id')
    region = entry.get('region', {})
    region_id = region.get('id')
    region_name = region.get('value')
    if code and region_id and region_id in {'EAS','ECS','LCN','MEA','NAC','SAS','SSF'}:
        iso3_to_region[code] = {'region_id': region_id, 'region_name': region_name}

# Filter countries to those present in WB mapping (strict WB classification)
filtered = []
for c in countries:
    if c['code'] in iso3_to_region:
        r = iso3_to_region[c['code']]
        filtered.append({**c, **r})

# Parse Region sheet totals for the 7 major regions
region_rows = region_json['sheets'][0]['data'][0]['rowData']
reg_header_cells = region_rows[0]['values']
reg_headers = [get_cell_value(c) for c in reg_header_cells]
try:
    ridx_code = reg_headers.index('Region Code')
    ridx_name = reg_headers.index('Region Name')
    ridx_gdp = reg_headers.index('Economy (millions of US dollars)')
except ValueError as e:
    raise SystemExit(f"Region header missing: {e} in {reg_headers}")

region_totals = {}
for row in region_rows[1:]:
    values = row.get('values', [])
    if not values:
        continue
    code = get_cell_value(values[ridx_code]) if ridx_code < len(values) else None
    name = get_cell_value(values[ridx_name]) if ridx_name < len(values) else None
    gdp = get_cell_value(values[ridx_gdp]) if ridx_gdp < len(values) else None
    if code in {'EAS','ECS','LCN','MEA','NAC','SAS','SSF'} and isinstance(gdp, (int,float)):
        region_totals[code] = {'name': name, 'gdp_musd': float(gdp)}

# Group countries by region
from collections import defaultdict
by_region = defaultdict(list)
for c in filtered:
    by_region[c['region_id']].append(c)

# Compute CR5 per region
results = []
for code in ['EAS','ECS','LCN','MEA','NAC','SAS','SSF']:
    countries_in_region = by_region.get(code, [])
    countries_in_region.sort(key=lambda x: x['gdp_musd'], reverse=True)
    top = countries_in_region[:5]
    top_names = [c['name'] for c in top]
    top_sum = sum(c['gdp_musd'] for c in top)
    reg_total = region_totals.get(code, {}).get('gdp_musd', 0.0)
    reg_name = region_totals.get(code, {}).get('name') or (countries_in_region[0]['region_name'] if countries_in_region else code)
    cr5_ratio = (top_sum / reg_total * 100.0) if reg_total else 0.0
    results.append({
        'Region': reg_name,
        'Top5_Countries': "/".join(top_names),
        'Top5_GDP_Sum': top_sum,
        'Region_GDP_Total': reg_total,
        'CR5_Ratio': cr5_ratio,
        'region_code': code,
        'country_count': len(countries_in_region)
    })

# Sort by descending CR5 ratio
results.sort(key=lambda x: x['CR5_Ratio'], reverse=True)

# Prepare values for writing
headers_out = ['Region','Top5_Countries','Top5_GDP_Sum','Region_GDP_Total','CR5_Ratio']
rows_out = []
for r in results:
    rows_out.append([
        r['Region'],
        r['Top5_Countries'],
        round(r['Top5_GDP_Sum'], 3),
        round(r['Region_GDP_Total'], 3),
        f"{r['CR5_Ratio']:.2f}%"
    ])

print(json.dumps({'headers': headers_out, 'rows': rows_out, 'debug': [{k: r[k] for k in ['region_code','country_count','CR5_Ratio']} for r in results]}, ensure_ascii=False))
 code
```

<div className="thinking-box">
🧐`Agent`

I have completed the CR5 analysis and saved the results to a new Google Spreadsheet.

What I did:
- Read GDP2022 data from your Google Sheet (Country and Region tabs).
- Mapped each country to a World Bank major region using the official WB country API, strictly following WB classifications.
- For each WB major region (East Asia & Pacific, Europe & Central Asia, Latin America & Caribbean, Middle East & North Africa, North America, South Asia, Sub-Saharan Africa):
  - Ranked member countries by 2022 GDP (in millions of USD).
  - Summed the top 5 countries’ GDP (or fewer if a region has fewer than 5 economies) and divided by the total regional GDP to get CR5, shown as a percentage rounded to two decimals.
- Created a new Google Spreadsheet named “GDP CR5 Analysis” and a table titled “gdp_cr5_analysis” with the requested headers and data, sorted by CR5 descending.

Spreadsheet:
- Title: GDP CR5 Analysis
- Sheet: gdp_cr5_analysis
- ID: 1o4yC0YhH3pmSg_MPKiT083TgiakO3WMZAPUwLcxbApY
